msg:Onion Butler added WeChat one day in advance and established a service WeChat group. Thirteen staff members serve customers. There should be shareholders or bosses in the group. They will see the service quality at any time and give thumbs up to the boss!
The butler provided a guide for the game, which was very detailed. We had a great time following the guide.
The location is in a village not far from the main road. It is very quiet. The pier is at the door. However, it has rained in the past two days and you cannot take a bamboo raft. You can see the landscape from the room, the rooftop of the hotel yard and the restaurant, and you can do it without leaving home. Enjoy the view.
We were upgraded to a room type free of charge. The view from the suite was great, and there were welcome fruits. The water dispenser was plugged into the mineral water to heat it up. It was very clean and avoided the need to boil the kettle.
Afternoon tea and breakfast are both very rich. Basque cake and black tea panna cotta are fragrant and not sweet, and taste great.
The whole yard is very delicate and quiet. In the morning, you can see the aunties carefully cleaning the glass and cleaning the swimming pool!
The lobby on the first floor has a reception area and a children's playroom with many board games to play.
It was very comfortable to lie down by the pool at night, it was quiet and there were no mosquitoes, it was very comfortable.
There is a dedicated parking lot and is self-driving friendly.
